<div class="section-heading page-width heading_4 mobile_heading_8">INGREDIENTS</div>
<div class="slider-enable slider-enable-template--16131941597341__58cdc12c-c834-4eb7-93f6-705135b5a44f">
<div class="collection--slider swiper-wrapper">
<div class="collection-item swiper-slide">
<a href="" style="text-decoration:none;">
<div class="collection-item-container">
<div class="collection-image">
<img src="//bhumi.com.au/cdn/shop/files/Bhumi_Organic_Cotton_Fairtrade_-_Organic_Cotton.jpg?v=1682120174" width="100%"/>
</div>
<div class="collection-title mobile_subheading_3 heading_4"> Organic Cotton </div>
<div class="collection-content body_2 mobile_body_7"><p>We start at the source: our cotton seeds are organic, not GMOs, and our farm partners rely exclusively on non-toxic resources to qualify as 100% organic.</p></div>
</div>
</a>
</div>
<div class="collection-item swiper-slide">
<a href="" style="text-decoration:none;">
<div class="collection-item-container">
<div class="collection-image">
<img src="//bhumi.com.au/cdn/shop/files/Bhumi_Organic_Cotton_Fairtrade_Rain_Water.jpg?v=1682121220" width="100%"/>
</div>
<div class="collection-title mobile_subheading_3 heading_4"> Rain water </div>
<div class="collection-content body_2 mobile_body_7"><p>We use harvested monsoon rain water throughout the entire seed to shelf journey to avoid wasting this precious natural resource.</p></div>
</div>
</a>
</div>
<div class="collection-item swiper-slide">
<a href="" style="text-decoration:none;">
<div class="collection-item-container">
<div class="collection-image">
<img src="//bhumi.com.au/cdn/shop/files/Bhumi_Organic_Cotton_Fairtrade_Dyes.jpg?v=1682122843" width="100%"/>
</div>
<div class="collection-title mobile_subheading_3 heading_4"> DYES </div>
<div class="collection-content body_2 mobile_body_7"><p>We use non toxic GOTS certified dyes. All our prints and fabrics are dyed using water based dyes free of ammonia, formaldehyde, chlorine bleach and toxic heavy metals. </p></div>
</div>
</a>
</div>
<div class="collection-item swiper-slide">
<a href="" style="text-decoration:none;">
<div class="collection-item-container">
<div class="collection-image">
<img src="//bhumi.com.au/cdn/shop/files/Bhumi_Organic_Cotton_Fairtrade_Potato_Starch.jpg?v=1682121446" width="100%"/>
</div>
<div class="collection-title mobile_subheading_3 heading_4"> Potato starch </div>
<div class="collection-content body_2 mobile_body_7"><p>Instead of using harsh toxic chemicals during production and finishing, we use potato starch to coat the threads which strengthens and prevents breakdown.</p></div>
</div>
</a>
</div>
<div class="collection-item swiper-slide">
<a href="" style="text-decoration:none;">
<div class="collection-item-container">
<div class="collection-image">
<img src="//bhumi.com.au/cdn/shop/files/Bhumi_Organic_Cotton_Fairtrade_Neem.jpg?v=1682122537" width="100%"/>
</div>
<div class="collection-title mobile_subheading_3 heading_4"> Neem </div>
<div class="collection-content body_2 mobile_body_7"><p>Using age old traditional farming practices we use Neem as an organic pest and fungal control for our crops instead of toxic insecticides or pesticides.</p></div>
</div>
</a>
</div>
<div class="collection-item swiper-slide">
<a href="" style="text-decoration:none;">
<div class="collection-item-container">
<div class="collection-image">
<img src="//bhumi.com.au/cdn/shop/files/Bhumi_Organic_Cotton_Fairtrade_Marigold.jpg?v=1682120955" width="100%"/>
</div>
<div class="collection-title mobile_subheading_3 heading_4"> Marigold </div>
<div class="collection-content body_2 mobile_body_7"><p>We work with nature to protect the land by using innovative natural pest control methods and the power of the humble marigold.</p></div>
</div>
</a>
</div>
<div class="collection-item swiper-slide">
<a href="" style="text-decoration:none;">
<div class="collection-item-container">

<div class="collection-title mobile_subheading_3 heading_4"> Solar Power </div>
<div class="collection-content body_2 mobile_body_7"><p>We use the power of the sun. Our mills harness the suns energy with on site solar plants.</p></div>

<div class="faq-container"><div class="faq">
<div class="rich-text__subheading mobile_title_1 subheading_11">
<p>WHY CHOOSE BHUMI?</p>
<svg fill="none" height="6" viewbox="0 0 9 6" width="9" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M8 1.25L4.5 4.75L1 1.25" stroke="#63666A" stroke-opacity="0.6"></path>
</svg>
</div>
<div class="rich-text__text rte text-797d4130-f25e-414b-9015-ad750bc63ab7 mobile_body_6 body_1">
<p>We can guarantee 100% certified organic products that do not harm the earth or Her people in any way. Using GOTS certified fairtrade cotton, we can promise zero toxic pesticides or dyes are used at any stage of our Seed to Shelf journey.</p>
</div>
</div><div class="faq">
<div class="rich-text__subheading mobile_title_1 subheading_11">
<p>WHERE DOES BHUMI SOURCE ORGANIC COTTON FROM?</p>
<svg fill="none" height="6" viewbox="0 0 9 6" width="9" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M8 1.25L4.5 4.75L1 1.25" stroke="#63666A" stroke-opacity="0.6"></path>
</svg>
</div>
<div class="rich-text__text rte text-f176dd0d-d3b6-4926-91ae-c3f293daf093 mobile_body_6 body_1">
<p>Currently Bhumi sources all of its organic cotton from India (and organic Linen from Belgium). India has one of the longest and respected textile traditions in the world, which means it provides us access to some of the highest quality production facilities in the world that comply with Global Organic Textile Standard (GOTS)Â and Soil Association requirements.</p>
</div>
</div><div class="faq">
<div class="rich-text__subheading mobile_title_1 subheading_11">
<p>WHAT ARE THE BENEFITS OF CHOOSING CERTIFIED ORGANIC COTTON?</p>
<svg fill="none" height="6" viewbox="0 0 9 6" width="9" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M8 1.25L4.5 4.75L1 1.25" stroke="#63666A" stroke-opacity="0.6"></path>
</svg>
</div>
<div class="rich-text__text rte text-27c6d516-55ac-482b-985e-3bee7c039b65 mobile_body_6 body_1">
<p>Not only does organic cotton have a low environmental impact, but it is also softer and more gentle and durable than standard cotton making it a natural choice for all our products. Choosing organic cotton brings the intrinsic beauty of nature into your home without the presence of any nasties (toxic chemicals, GMO, etc.) and allows you to enjoy the purest form of cotton as nature intended it to be ...and knowing it was ethically made inÂ adherence to the strictest environmental standards.</p>
</div>
</div></div>

We recognise and honour the ongoing connection and deep spiritual relationship that Aboriginal and Torres Strait Islander peoples have to Australian Country, and acknowledge the unique role they play in caring for and protecting it for future generations. We demonstrate our respect for First Nations peoples through our commitments to environmentally sustainable and ethical business practices. We recognise their continuing connection to land and waters, and thank them for protecting our natural resources and ecosystems.
